add_namespace = amcivwar

country_event = { # Jack Reed declares the seccession of the CSA as an independent state
	id = amcivwar.1
	title = amcivwar.1.t
	desc = amcivwar.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_finnish_pact
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		add_popularity = { ideology = syndicalist popularity = -0.3 }
        remove_ideas = new_year_strike
		remove_ideas = max_schachtman
		remove_ideas = paul_mattick
		remove_ideas = william_foster
		remove_ideas = reed_nat_oil
		CSA = {
			transfer_state = 395
			transfer_state = 393
			transfer_state = 394
			transfer_state = 358
			transfer_state = 396
			transfer_state = 261
			transfer_state = 360
			transfer_state = 359

			add_state_core = 395
			add_state_core = 393
			add_state_core = 394
			add_state_core = 358
			add_state_core = 396
			add_state_core = 261
			add_state_core = 360
			add_state_core = 359

			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = amcivwar.341 days = 0 }
			}
		}
        #End Guarantee on legation cities
		add_political_power = 160
		add_manpower = -100000
		if = { limit = { has_country_flag = REED_PRES } country_event = { id = amcivwar.32 } }
	    if = { limit = { 391 = { is_owned_by = USA } has_government = paternal_autocratist } country_event = { id = amcivwar.9001 days = 1 } }
	}

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		add_popularity = { ideology = syndicalist popularity = -0.3 }
        remove_ideas = new_year_strike
		remove_ideas = max_schachtman
		remove_ideas = paul_mattick
		remove_ideas = william_foster
		remove_ideas = reed_nat_oil
		CSA = {
			transfer_state = 395
			transfer_state = 393
			transfer_state = 394
			transfer_state = 358
			transfer_state = 396
			transfer_state = 261
			transfer_state = 360
			transfer_state = 359

			add_state_core = 395
			add_state_core = 393
			add_state_core = 394
			add_state_core = 358
			add_state_core = 396
			add_state_core = 261
			add_state_core = 360
			add_state_core = 359

			change_tag_from = USA

			hidden_effect = { 
				country_event = { id = amcivwar.341 days = 0 }
			}
		}

		#End Guarantee on legation cities
		add_political_power = 160
		add_manpower = -100000
		if = { limit = { has_country_flag = REED_PRES } country_event = { id = amcivwar.32 } }
		if = { limit = { 391 = { is_owned_by = USA } has_government = paternal_autocratist } country_event = { id = amcivwar.9001 days = 1 } }
	}
	
	
}

country_event = { # Long launches major protests in the South
	id = amcivwar.2
	title = amcivwar.2.t
	desc = amcivwar.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = amcivwar.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocratist popularity = -0.3 }
		remove_ideas = southern_rally
		remove_ideas = long_agg_ref
        remove_ideas = long_mod_ref
		remove_ideas = long_lim_ref
		remove_ideas = long_agreff
		remove_ideas = long_tariff
		remove_ideas = long_no_tariff
		TEX = {
			transfer_state = 365
			transfer_state = 367
			transfer_state = 370
			transfer_state = 364

			add_state_core = 365
			add_state_core = 367
			add_state_core = 370
			add_state_core = 364

			hidden_effect = { USA = { country_event = { id = amcivwar.3 days = 1 }
			if = { limit = { has_government = syndicalist } country_event = { id = amcivwar.3000 days = 1 } } } }

			hidden_effect = { 
				TEX = { 
					country_event = { id = amcivwar.341 days = 0 } 
				}
			}
		}

		add_political_power = 160
		add_manpower = -100000
		if = { limit = { has_country_flag = LONG_PRES } country_event = { id = amcivwar.8 } }
	}

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocratist popularity = -0.3 }
        remove_ideas = southern_rally
		remove_ideas = long_agg_ref
        remove_ideas = long_mod_ref
		remove_ideas = long_lim_ref
		remove_ideas = long_agreff
		remove_ideas = long_tariff
		remove_ideas = long_no_tariff
		TEX = {
			transfer_state = 365
			transfer_state = 367
			transfer_state = 370
			transfer_state = 364

			add_state_core = 365
			add_state_core = 367
			add_state_core = 370
			add_state_core = 364
			
			change_tag_from = USA }

			hidden_effect = { USA = { country_event = { id = amcivwar.3 days = 1 }
			if = { limit = { has_government = syndicalist } country_event = { id = amcivwar.3000 days = 1 } } } }

			hidden_effect = { 
				TEX = { 
					country_event = { id = amcivwar.341 days = 0 } 
				}
			}
		

		add_political_power = 160
		add_manpower = -100000
		if = { limit = { has_country_flag = LONG_PRES } country_event = { id = amcivwar.8 } }
	}

}

country_event = { # California leaves the Union
	id = amcivwar.4
	title = amcivwar.4.t
	desc = amcivwar.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = amcivwar.4.a
        ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		CAL = {

			transfer_state = 386
			transfer_state = 385
			transfer_state = 378
			transfer_state = 797
			transfer_state = 798

			add_state_core = 386
			add_state_core = 385
			add_state_core = 378
			add_state_core = 797
			add_state_core = 798

			add_political_power = 160
			add_manpower = -100000

			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = amcivwar.341 days = 0 } }
		}
		hidden_effect = { if = { limit = { 379 = { is_owned_by = USA }
		OR = { has_government = syndicalist has_government = paternal_autocratist } } country_event = { id = amcivwar.5 days = 2 } }
		if = { limit = { 387 = { is_owned_by = USA }
		OR = { has_government = syndicalist has_government = paternal_autocratist } } country_event = { id = amcivwar.6 days = 2 } } }
	}

	option = {
		name = amcivwar.4.b
        ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		CAL = {

			transfer_state = 386
			transfer_state = 385
			transfer_state = 378
			transfer_state = 797
			transfer_state = 798

			add_state_core = 386
			add_state_core = 385
			add_state_core = 378
			add_state_core = 797
			add_state_core = 798

			change_tag_from = USA

			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = amcivwar.341 days = 0 } }
		}

		add_political_power = 160
		add_manpower = -100000
		hidden_effect = { if = { limit = { 379 = { is_owned_by = USA }
		OR = { has_government = syndicalist has_government = paternal_autocratist } } country_event = { id = amcivwar.5 days = 2 } }
		if = { limit = { 387 = { is_owned_by = USA }
		OR = { has_government = syndicalist has_government = paternal_autocratist } } country_event = { id = amcivwar.6 days = 2 } } }
	}

}

country_event = { # USA Junta under MacArthur
	id = amcivwar.7
	title = amcivwar.7.t
	desc = amcivwar.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_global_flag = ACW_JUNTA
	}
	
	option = {
		name = amcivwar.7.a

		hidden_effect = {
		add_popularity = {
            ideology = totalist
            popularity = -1
        }
		add_popularity = {
            ideology = radical_socialist
            popularity = -1
        }
		add_popularity = {
            ideology = syndicalist
            popularity = -1
        }
		add_popularity = {
            ideology = social_democratist
            popularity = -1
        }
        add_popularity = {
            ideology = social_liberalist
            popularity = -1
        }
        add_popularity = {
            ideology = market_liberalist
            popularity = -1
        }
        add_popularity = {
            ideology = social_conservatist
            popularity = -1
        }
        add_popularity = {
            ideology = authoritarian_democratist
            popularity = -1
        }
        add_popularity = {
            ideology = paternal_autocratist
            popularity = -1
        }
        add_popularity = {
            ideology = national_populist
            popularity = -1
        }
        }

        add_popularity = {
            ideology = authoritarian_democratist
            popularity = 0.2
        }
        add_popularity = {
            ideology = market_liberalist
            popularity = 0.4
        }
        add_popularity = {
            ideology = social_liberalist
            popularity = 0.4
        }

		set_politics = { ruling_party = authoritarian_democratist elections_allowed = no }

		hidden_effect = { retire_country_leader = yes }

		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Douglas MacArthur"
			desc = "MACARTHUR_DESC"
			picture = "Portrait_USA_Douglas_MacArthur.dds"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = authoritarian_democratist_subtype
			traits = {}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
		remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
        remove_ideas_with_trait = foreign_minister
        remove_ideas_with_trait = economy_minister
        remove_ideas_with_trait = intel_minister
        }

		set_country_flag = MACARTHUR_HOS

        add_ideas = {
        	USA_George_Van_Horn_Moseley_hog_ade
        	USA_Cordell_Hull_for_sli
        	USA_Henry_Morgenthau_eco_sde
        	USA_Ray_L_Wilbur_int_mli
        }
        
		set_capital = 382
	}
}

country_event = { # Occupy New England 
	id = amcivwar.10
	title = amcivwar.10.t
	desc = amcivwar.10.d
	picture = GFX_Amcivwar_generic4
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = CAN 
		#CAN = { is_ai = yes } #REVIST Fires for ai until/unless it can be taught to manage focuses better
		country_exists = CSA
		country_exists = USA
		USA = { 
			has_defensive_war_with = CSA
		}
		357 = { is_owned_by = USA }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = amcivwar.10.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 85
		}

		add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = occupied_new_england }
		hidden_effect = { USA = { country_event = { id = amcivwar.11 days = 1 }}}
		hidden_effect = { CSA = { country_event = { id = amcivwar.34 days = 1 }}}
		hidden_effect = { TEX = { country_event = { id = amcivwar.35 days = 1 }}}
	 	add_state_claim = 357
		set_global_flag = amcivwar_10
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = SCHEME_1_BYPASS }
	}

	# option = { 
		# name = amcivwar.10.b

		# ai_chance = {
			# factor = 1
		# }

		# declare_war_on = { target = CSA type = annex_everything	}
		# add_political_power = -50
		# set_global_flag = amcivwar_10	
	# }

	option = { 
	 	name = amcivwar.10.c

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 14
		}

		add_political_power = -20	
		set_global_flag = amcivwar_10
	}		
}

country_event = { # Occupy Alaska
	id = amcivwar.12
	title = amcivwar.12.t
	desc = amcivwar.12.d
	picture = GFX_Amcivwar_alaska
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = CAN
		#CAN = { is_ai = yes } #REVIST Fires for ai until/unless it can be taught to manage focuses better
		country_exists = CSA
		country_exists = USA
		USA = { 
			has_defensive_war_with = CSA
		}
		463 = { is_owned_by = USA }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = amcivwar.12.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}

		add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = occupied_alaska_CAN }
		hidden_effect = { USA = { country_event = { id = amcivwar.13 days = 1 }}}
		hidden_effect = { CSA = { country_event = { id = amcivwar.36 days = 1 }}}
		hidden_effect = { TEX = { country_event = { id = amcivwar.37 days = 1 }}}
		hidden_effect = { CAL = { country_event = { id = amcivwar.38 days = 1 }}}
		set_global_flag = ACW_CAN_SEIZE_ALASKA
	}

	option = { 
		name = amcivwar.12.b

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		add_political_power = -20
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { CAL = { has_war_with = USA }}}

			hidden_effect = { CAL = { country_event = { id = amcivwar.39 days = 1 }}}
		}	 	
	}		
}

country_event = { # California has a chance to declare war.
	id = amcivwar.18
	title = amcivwar.18.t
	desc = amcivwar.18.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = CAL
		country_exists = USA
		is_puppet = no
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = USA
			is_in_faction_with = USA
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = amcivwar.18.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}

		declare_war_on = { target = USA type = civil_war_focus }
	}

	option = { 
		name = amcivwar.18.b

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}

		add_political_power = 20
		set_country_flag = amcivwar.18	
	}		
}

country_event = { #  Responds to PSA's alliance with him
	id = amcivwar.47
	title = amcivwar.47.t
	desc = amcivwar.47.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { 
		name = amcivwar.47.a

		USA = {	
			remove_state_core = 386
			remove_state_core = 385
			remove_state_core = 378
			remove_state_core = 797
			remove_state_core = 798
			set_global_flag = CAL_Allies_USA

			if = {
				limit = {
					CAL = { owns_state = 379 }
				}

				remove_state_core = 379
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					CAL = { owns_state = 387 }
				}

				remove_state_core = 387
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					USA = { has_war_with = CSA }
				}

				CAL = { add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = USA enemy = CSA }}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					USA = { has_war_with = TEX }
				}

				CAL = { add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = USA enemy = TEX }}
			}
		}
		
		create_faction = "American Alliance"
		add_to_faction = CAL
	}						
}

					CSA = { has_war_with = USA }
				}

			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					CSA = { has_war_with = TEX }
				}

				CAL = { add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = CSA enemy = TEX }}
			}
		}
		
		create_faction = "American Alliance"
		add_to_faction = CAL
	}						
}

		tag = CAN
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = USA
			has_war_with = TEX
			has_war_with = CSA
			country_exists = NEE
			is_puppet = yes
		}	
		357 = { is_owned_by = CAN }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = amcivwar.123.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}

		add_political_power = 20

		NEE = {
			transfer_state = 357
			transfer_state = 796

			add_state_core = 357
			add_state_core = 796

			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = amcivwar.125 days = 2 }}
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = amcivwar.341 days = 0 } }
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = amcivwar.123.b

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}

		add_political_power = 20

		NEE = {
			transfer_state = 357
			transfer_state = 796

			add_state_core = 357
			add_state_core = 796

			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = amcivwar.125 days = 2 }}
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = amcivwar.341 days = 0 } }
			change_tag_from = CAN
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = amcivwar.123.c

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 9
		}

		add_state_claim = 357

		set_country_flag = CANOCCNE
	}		
}

country_event = { # 1939
	id = amcivwar.138
	title = amcivwar.138.t
	desc = amcivwar.138.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
         tag = NEE
		AND = {
			OR = { 
				has_government = social_liberalist
				has_government = social_liberalist
				has_government = market_liberalist
				has_government = social_conservatist
			}
		}
		date > 1939.4.19	
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = amcivwar.138.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}

		hidden_effect = {
		add_popularity = {
            ideology = totalist
            popularity = -1
        }
		add_popularity = {
            ideology = radical_socialist
            popularity = -1
        }
		add_popularity = {
            ideology = syndicalist
            popularity = -1
        }
		add_popularity = {
            ideology = social_democratist
            popularity = -1
        }
        add_popularity = {
            ideology = social_liberalist
            popularity = -1
        }
        add_popularity = {
            ideology = market_liberalist
            popularity = -1
        }
        add_popularity = {
            ideology = social_conservatist
            popularity = -1
        }
        add_popularity = {
            ideology = authoritarian_democratist
            popularity = -1
        }
        add_popularity = {
            ideology = paternal_autocratist
            popularity = -1
        }
        add_popularity = {
            ideology = national_populist
            popularity = -1
        }
        }

        add_popularity = {
            ideology = social_conservatist
            popularity = 0.4
        }
        add_popularity = {
            ideology = market_liberalist
            popularity = 0.3
        }
        add_popularity = {
            ideology = social_liberalist
            popularity = 0.3
        }

		set_politics = { ruling_party = social_conservatist elections_allowed = no }

		retire_country_leader = yes

		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Percival P. Baxter"
			desc = "BAXTER_DESC"
			picture = "Portrait_NEE_Percival_P_Baxter.dds"

		tag = CAN
		owns_state = 463
		date > 1939.5.1	
	}

		days = 1
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = amcivwar.141.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}

		add_manpower = -2000
		add_resource = { type = oil amount = 12 state = 463 }

	}	

	option = { 
		name = amcivwar.141.b

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}

		add_resource = { type = oil amount = 1 state = 463 }
	}

country_event = { # The Territory of Hawaii Revolts
	id = amcivwar.142
	title = amcivwar.142.t
	desc = amcivwar.142.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		country_exists = CAL
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = amcivwar.142.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}

		add_political_power = 60

		HAW = {
			transfer_state = 629

			add_state_core = 629

			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = amcivwar.143 days = 2 }}
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = amcivwar.144 days = 4 }}
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = amcivwar.341 days = 0 } }
		}	
	}

	option = { 
		name = amcivwar.142.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}

		add_political_power = 60

		HAW = {
			transfer_state = 629

			add_state_core = 629

			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = amcivwar.143 days = 2 }}
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = amcivwar.144 days = 4 }}
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = amcivwar.341 days = 0 } }

			change_tag_from = USA
		}	
	}		
}

country_event = { # Commune of France volunteers
	id = amcivwar.273
	title = amcivwar.273.t
	desc = amcivwar.273.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = FRA
		country_exists = CSA
		has_war = no
		OR = {
			has_government = totalist
			has_government = radical_socialist
			has_government = syndicalist
		}
		CSA = { controls_state = 358 }
		CSA = { has_war = yes }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = amcivwar.273.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}

		add_manpower = -10000

		send_equipment = {
            target = CSA
            type = infantry_equipment
            amount = 1000
        }

        hidden_effect = { CSA = { country_event = { id = amcivwar.276 days = 1 }}}
	}

	option = { 
		name = amcivwar.273.b

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}

		send_equipment = {
            target = CSA
            type = infantry_equipment
            amount = 1000
        }

        hidden_effect = { CSA = { country_event = { id = amcivwar.289 days = 1 }}}
	}

	option = { 
		name = amcivwar.273.c

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
		}

		add_political_power = -60
	}		
}

############ CSA Cities
### Detroid

country_event = {
	id = amcivwar.305
	title = amcivwar.305.t
	desc = amcivwar.305.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			and = {
				tag = USA
				controls_state = 393
				has_war_with = CSA
				NOT = { has_global_flag = CAP_DET_USA }
			}
		}		
		OR = {
			and = {
				tag = TEX
				controls_state = 393
				has_war_with = CSA
				NOT = { has_global_flag = CAP_DET_TEX }
			}
		}
		OR = {
			and = {
				tag = CAL
				controls_state = 393
				has_war_with = CSA
				NOT = { has_global_flag = CAP_DET_CAL }
			}
		}

		CSA = { owns_state = 393 }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = amcivwar.305.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 65
		}

		remove_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 state = 393 }
		add_political_power = 20

        if = {
        	limit = { tag = CAL }

        	set_global_flag = CAP_DET_CAL
        }

        if = {
        	limit = { tag = USA }

        	set_global_flag = CAP_DET_USA
        }

        if = {
        	limit = { tag = TEX }

        	set_global_flag = CAP_DET_TEX
        }
	}

	option = { 
		name = amcivwar.305.b

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 35
		}

		add_political_power = -20

        if = {
        	limit = { tag = CAL }

        	set_global_flag = CAP_DET_CAL
        }

        if = {
        	limit = { tag = USA }

        	set_global_flag = CAP_DET_USA
        }

        if = {
        	limit = { tag = TEX }

        	set_global_flag = CAP_DET_TEX
        }
	}		
}

	id = amcivwar.306
	title = amcivwar.306.t
	desc = amcivwar.306.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers
	
	fire_only_once = yes

		TAG = CSA

		has_global_flag = CAP_DET_CAL
		NOT = { has_global_flag = CAP_DET_2 }

		days = 0

country_event = { 
	id = amcivwar.341
	title = amcivwar.341.t
	desc = amcivwar.341.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	hidden = yes
	
	option = {
		name = amcivwar.341.a
		hidden_effect = {
		### Air doctrines ####
			if = {
				limit = {USA = {has_tech = air_superiority} }
				 set_technology = { air_superiority  = 1 } 
			}
		###
			if = {
				limit = {USA = {has_tech = infrastructure_destruction} }
				set_technology = { infrastructure_destruction  = 1 }
			}
		###	
			if = {
				limit = {USA = {has_tech = home_defence} }
				set_technology = { home_defence  = 1 }
			}
		###	
			if = {
				limit = {USA = {has_tech = naval_strike_tactics} }
				set_technology = { naval_strike_tactics  = 1 }
			}
		###
			if = {
				limit = {USA = {has_tech = fighter_sweeps} }
				set_technology = { fighter_sweeps  = 1 }
			}
		###
			if = {
				limit = {USA = {has_tech = dogfighting_experience} }
				set_technology = { dogfighting_experience  = 1 }
			}
		###
